Attached you will find the final version of the logo. Please feel free to
use it wherever you like when referring to Singularity!

Also, the base support for Docker integration is working as follows:

$ singularity shell docker://ubuntu:latest
$ singularity import /path/to/container.img docker://centos:latest
$ singularity bootstrap /path/to/container.img docker.def

And inside that docker.def:

BootStrap: docker
From: ubuntu:latest
IncludeCmd: yes

There are still some minor cleanups to be done to the code, but all of this
is available to test and play with in the master branch! Thank you Vanessa
for the fantastic work figuring out the largely undocumented/misdocumented
Docker API!

I am expecting to lock the master branch to feature additions by the end of
this week... Cleanups and bug fixes over next week, and the release near
end of the month. The feature list for 2.2 is seriously quite amazing, you
are gonna love it!

-- 
Gregory M. Kurtzer
HPC Systems Architect and Technology Developer
Lawrence Berkeley National Laboratory HPCS
University of California Berkeley Research IT
Singularity Linux Containers (http://singularity.lbl.gov/)
Warewulf Cluster Management (http://warewulf.lbl.gov/)
GitHub: https://github.com/gmkurtzer, Twitter: https://twitter.com/gmkurtzer
